COMPRESSOR AND ACCESSORIES)","Milestones","NS",0.0,"2026-11-13","2026-11-13",0.0,1,"FM"]]};
const F = RAW.fields;
const idx = {}; F.forEach((f,i)=>idx[f]=i);
const STATUS_LABEL = {NS:'Not Started', IP:'In Progress', C:'Completed'};

document.getElementById('tbProject').textContent = RAW.project_name + ' — TFT II / TFT SUD Catch-up Plan';
document.getElementById('tbDate').textContent = RAW.data_date;
document.getElementById('tbCount').textContent = RAW.tasks.length.toLocaleString();

// ---------- KPIs ----------
const tasks = RAW.tasks;
const total = tasks.length;
let sumPct=0, done=0, prog=0, ns=0, crit=0;
const discMap = {}; // name -> {total, done, prog, ns, sumPct}
tasks.forEach(t=>{
  const disc=t[idx.discipline], status=t[idx.status], pct=t[idx.pct], driving=t[idx.driving];
  sumPct += pct;
  if(status==='C') done++;
  else if(status==='IP') prog++;
  else ns++;
  if(driving===1) crit++;
  if(!discMap[disc]) discMap[disc] = {total:0, done:0, prog:0, ns:0, sumPct:0};
  const d = discMap[disc];
  d.total++; d.sumPct += pct;
  if(status==='C') d.done++; else if(status==='IP') d.prog++; else d.ns++;
});
const avgPct = (sumPct/total).toFixed(1);

document.getElementById('kTotal').textContent = total.toLocaleString();
document.getElementById('kPct').textContent = avgPct + '%';
document.getElementById('kPctSub').textContent = done.toLocaleString()+' of '+total.toLocaleString()+' fully complete';
document.getElementById('kDone').textContent = done.toLocaleString();
document.getElementById('kProg').textContent = prog.toLocaleString();
document.getElementById('kNs').textContent = ns.toLocaleString();
document.getElementById('kCrit').textContent = crit.toLocaleString();

// ---------- Status chart ----------
new Chart(document.getElementById('statusChart'), {
  type: 'doughnut',
  data: {
    labels: ['Completed','In Progress','Not Started'],
    datasets: [{
      data: [done, prog, ns],
      backgroundColor: ['#3FB081','#E8A33D','#23364A'],
      borderColor: '#101E2E',
      borderWidth: 3,
    }]
  },
  options: {
    responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false,
    plugins:{
      legend:{position:'bottom', labels:{color:'#85A0B8', font:{family:"'IBM Plex Mono'", size:11}, padding:14}},
      tooltip:{callbacks:{label:(c)=>` ${c.label}: ${c.parsed.toLocaleString()} (${(c.parsed/total*100).toFixed(1)}%)`}}
    },
    cutout:'62%'
  }
});

// ---------- Discipline list (custom stacked bars) ----------
const discEntries = Object.entries(discMap).sort((a,b)=>b[1].total-a[1].total);
const maxDiscTotal = discEntries[0][1].total;
const discListEl = document.getElementById('discList');
discEntries.forEach(([name, d])=>{
  const w = (d.total/maxDiscTotal*100).toFixed(1);
  const pDone = (d.done/d.total*100).toFixed(2);
  const pProg = (d.prog/d.total*100).toFixed(2);
  const pNs = (d.ns/d.total*100).toFixed(2);
  const row = document.createElement('div');
  row.className='disc-row';
  row.innerHTML = `
    <div class="disc-name" title="${name}">${name}</div>
    <div class="disc-track" style="width:${w}%">
      <div class="disc-seg done" style="width:${pDone}%"></div>
      <div class="disc-seg prog" style="width:${pProg}%"></div>
      <div class="disc-seg ns" style="width:${pNs}%"></div>
    </div>
    <div class="disc-count">${d.total}</div>
  `;
  discListEl.appendChild(row);
});

// populate discipline filter
const discFilterEl = document.getElementById('discFilter');
discEntries.forEach(([name])=>{
  const opt = document.createElement('option');
  opt.value=name; opt.textContent=name;
  discFilterEl.appendChild(opt);
});

// ---------- Table: filter / sort / paginate ----------
let state = { search:'', disc:'', status:'', crit:'', sortKey:'code', sortDir:1, page:0, pageSize:50 };

function applyFilters(){
  let rows = tasks;
  if(state.disc) rows = rows.filter(t=>t[idx.discipline]===state.disc);
  if(state.status) rows = rows.filter(t=>t[idx.status]===state.status);
  if(state.crit) rows = rows.filter(t=>String(t[idx.driving])===state.crit);
  if(state.search){
    const s = state.search.toLowerCase();
    rows = rows.filter(t=> t[idx.code].toLowerCase().includes(s) || t[idx.name].toLowerCase().includes(s));
  }
  const key = idx[state.sortKey];
  rows = rows.slice().sort((a,b)=>{
    let av=a[key], bv=b[key];
    if(typeof av === 'string') av = av.toLowerCase();
    if(typeof bv === 'string') bv = bv.toLowerCase();
    if(av===null) av = -Infinity; if(bv===null) bv = -Infinity;
    if(av<bv) return -1*state.sortDir;
    if(av>bv) return 1*state.sortDir;
    return 0;
  });
  return rows;
}

function renderTable(){
  const rows = applyFilters();
  const pageCount = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(rows.length/state.pageSize));
  if(state.page >= pageCount) state.page = pageCount-1;
  if(state.page < 0) state.page = 0;
  const start = state.page*state.pageSize;
  const pageRows = rows.slice(start, start+state.pageSize);

  document.getElementById('resultCount').textContent = rows.length.toLocaleString()+' activities';
  document.getElementById('pagerInfo').textContent = `Page ${state.page+1} of ${pageCount}  ·  showing ${pageRows.length ? start+1 : 0}–${start+pageRows.length} of ${rows.length.toLocaleString()}`;
  document.getElementById('prevBtn').disabled = state.page<=0;
  document.getElementById('nextBtn').disabled = state.page>=pageCount-1;

  const tbody = document.getElementById('tableBody');
  tbody.innerHTML = pageRows.map(t=>{
    const code=t[idx.code], name=t[idx.name], disc=t[idx.discipline], status=t[idx.status],
          pct=t[idx.pct], start_d=t[idx.start]||'—', finish=t[idx.finish]||'—', driving=t[idx.driving];
    return `<tr>
      <td class="code">${code}</td>
      <td class="name">${name}${driving? '<span class="crit-flag">● CP</span>':''}</td>
      <td class="disc">${disc}</td>
      <td><span class="status-tag ${status}">${STATUS_LABEL[status]||status}</span></td>
      <td class="pct">${pct.toFixed(0)}%<span class="pct-bar-mini"><i style="width:${pct}%"></i></span></td>
      <td class="dates">${start_d}</td>
      <td class="dates">${finish}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');

  // sort header indicator
  document.querySelectorAll('thead th').forEach(th=>{
    th.classList.remove('sorted');
    const arrow = th.querySelector('.arrow');
    arrow.textContent='';
    if(th.dataset.key===state.sortKey){
      th.classList.add('sorted');
      arrow.textContent = state.sortDir===1 ? '▲' : '▼';
    }
  });
}

document.getElementById('searchBox').addEventListener('input', e=>{state.search=e.target.value; state.page=0; renderTable();});
document.getElementById('discFilter').addEventListener('change', e=>{state.disc=e.target.value; state.page=0; renderTable();});
document.getElementById('statusFilter').addEventListener('change', e=>{state.status=e.target.value; state.page=0; renderTable();});
document.getElementById('critFilter').addEventListener('change', e=>{state.crit=e.target.value; state.page=0; renderTable();});
document.getElementById('resetBtn').addEventListener('click', ()=>{
  state = {...state, search:'', disc:'', status:'', crit:'', page:0};
  document.getElementById('searchBox').value='';
  document.getElementById('discFilter').value='';
  document.getElementById('statusFilter').value='';
  document.getElementById('critFilter').value='';
  renderTable();
});
document.getElementById('prevBtn').addEventListener('click', ()=>{state.page--; renderTable();});
document.getElementById('nextBtn').addEventListener('click', ()=>{state.page++; renderTable();});
document.querySelectorAll('thead th').forEach(th=>{
  th.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
    const key = th.dataset.key;
    if(state.sortKey===key) state.sortDir*=-1;
    else { state.sortKey=key; state.sortDir=1; }
    renderTable();
  });
});

renderTable();
</script>
</body>
</html>
